  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5b792e42-dc3e-47ab-be23-6ad2982b7f02'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer13080186799337931038"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>Damn! I can’t believe I enjoyed it that much! It’s been a while since I read a fantasy book. Yes, I had had read a vampiry book recently (months ago) but a story with vampires, damons, witches, shapeshifters... I can’t even remember when was my last fantasy book! I loved this one!   <span id="freeText13080186799337931038" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br /><br />Damn! I can’t believe I enjoyed it that much! It’s been a while since I read a fantasy book. Yes, I had had read a vampiry book recently (months ago) but a story with vampires, damons, witches, shapeshifters... I can’t even remember when was my last fantasy book! I loved this one! I was hooked from the first chapter and with each chapter it got better! I loved Matthew so much; he was brave, smart, curious, caring… and I hated Tarrick! At first I had a mild hatred for him but chapter by chapter my hatred increased! He doesn’t deserve Matthew. I know he had reasons for what he did to Matthew but still I can’t accept them. I hope Matthew choose someone better than Tarrick, someone who really care for him and deserve his love and someone who chose something other than torturing as a help to him! maybe if there was Tarrick’s POV I could have understood him more. I hope I like him more in book two! Told in single POV, 3rd person. It was well-written and a bit slow but I didn’t mind it. It’s the first installment in the "Beautiful Monsters" series and it’s cliffy (but not a huge one). Overall, loved it and hope you enjoy it as well. Onto the second book!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1295787718949839815">Suddenly, I’m transported to an alternative universe where vampires, incubi, demons, gargoyles and uncountable supernatural species exist. 😱 Or may be not! 😂 We still don’t know if they don’t exist for real or not. 😁 So let me tell you one thing, this is not a romance novel. It might seem it is but it really is not. For all to start, there’s only one MC here, Matthew, the creature of both a vampire and an incubus. And this is about him and how he became what he is. 😌<br/><br/> <br/>Matthew, a 7 years old vampi</span>
  <span id="freeText1295787718949839815" style="display:none">Suddenly, I’m transported to an alternative universe where vampires, incubi, demons, gargoyles and uncountable supernatural species exist. 😱 Or may be not! 😂 We still don’t know if they don’t exist for real or not. 😁 So let me tell you one thing, this is not a romance novel. It might seem it is but it really is not. For all to start, there’s only one MC here, Matthew, the creature of both a vampire and an incubus. And this is about him and how he became what he is. 😌<br /><br /> <br />Matthew, a 7 years old vampire, who died for the first time when he was 32. Abandoned by his sire, he’s been on his own for 7 lone years. One day, he was attracted by an unusual thumping sensation and he was drawn to it like a moth to a flame. Little did he knew, he fell to the grasp of Tarrick, the high lord general of Incubi, and became a slave. And thus his story began. 😉 Along his journey as a slave and a prisoner of Incubi, he learnt that he’s not only a vampire but also a born incubus. He doesn’t wanna kneel in front of anyone but Tarrick broke him slowly and deceptively. He’s in a dilemma, does he belong to vampires or incubi? Whom should he pledge his fidelity to? 😐 And while Matthew is being very careful not to fall for handsome, irresistible General Tarrick, he belatedly realized that he’s already hopelessly fallen in love with Tarrick. 😒 While he once wanted more than anything to kill and destroy Tarrick, the man who broke his body and his soul, now he’d do anything and I mean anything to please and pleasure his lover. But his endeavor and loyalty were not appreciated and the High King of Incubi decided that he shouldn’t be more than just a tool in the centuries long war of vampires and incubi. And to worsen his misery, he realized that Tarrick never cared for him and manipulated him all along to achieve what he wanted. 😤 Broken, abandoned, lonely and miserable. 💔 How is Matthew going to survive and overcome everything? 😭<br /> <br /><br /><br /><b>I love Matthew .. obviously. 😁 His character is really fascinating and mysterious. There’s so much mystery about his past and how he became what he is to be. A true creature of enigma and puzzlement. 😉 And his mind is always in a battle of being a vampire and an incubus. Despite being a vampire, he doesn’t enjoy kill and he’s afraid of the monster that he has become. While, I’m not a big fan of how he got cheated, played and manipulated by those goddamn Incubi, I’m proud of the man Matthew has become. He was just a man who wanted someone and a society to belong to. 😭 He has a long journey ahead and I can’t wait to read more of his adventures. 😍 And surprise, surprise, surprise, that bastard Tarrick, I wanna flay him alive and kick him in the nuts! 🤬 How could he break my poor Matthew’s heart? After everything he has done for him and saved his sorry ass! Grrrrghhhhhhh! So frustrating. 😤 And so many interesting side characters. I’m especially intrigued by Lady Rosaline. I can’t wait to read more about her in the next issues in the series. This was a very enjoyable read. 😊👏 There were occasional MF scenes in the book but I didn’t mind since they were super erotic. 😜 And although this is particularly not about romance, you are in for a treat of those delicious erotic smut since those Incubi rut like mad. Love it! 😁😍<br /> <br /><br /><br />Favorite excerpts from the novel: 💙💚💜<br /><br /><i>They fought. They screamed. They begged. They died. And he loved it. And he hated himself for loving it.<br /><br />He was made to be a conqueror, he could feel it in his bones, and one day they would all see it when he forced them all to their knees before him.<br /><br />“I know my position might seem harsh, but always remember that even I have people I kneel before and must give my allegiance to. Collar or no, we all have our masters.”<br /><br />One day, that would be different for Matthew. One day, others would kneel before him.<br /><br />“Because love is the easiest way to control someone and I needed a way to control you.”</i><br /> <br /><br /><br />4.5 super sexy wings and tails and horns and fangs stars</b><br />⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️💫</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2302467140" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8302974517387645878"><b>4,25 STARS</b><br/><br/>Wow this book! This story! <br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/15423679.Jex_Lane' title='Jex Lane' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jex Lane</a> created such a unique and fantastic world with vampires, incubi, witches and so many scary creatures. And all together gave us a great story. <br/><br/>I've started this book right before going to sleep. Wrong choice! I just couldn't go to sleep until I finished it, at 5 AM. And now I'm at work, exhausted but I'm still thinking about this story! That's how much I enjoyed it. <br/><br/>I'll start by saying I'm NOT a fan of fantasy. But I've read some stories with vampire</span>
  <span id="freeText8302974517387645878" style="display:none"><b>4,25 STARS</b><br /><br />Wow this book! This story! <br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/15423679.Jex_Lane" title="Jex Lane" rel="nofollow noopener">Jex Lane</a> created such a unique and fantastic world with vampires, incubi, witches and so many scary creatures. And all together gave us a great story. <br /><br />I've started this book right before going to sleep. Wrong choice! I just couldn't go to sleep until I finished it, at 5 AM. And now I'm at work, exhausted but I'm still thinking about this story! That's how much I enjoyed it. <br /><br />I'll start by saying I'm NOT a fan of fantasy. But I've read some stories with vampires and I absolutely loved The Black Dagger Brotherhood by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/20248.J_R__Ward" title="J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">J.R. Ward</a>. Actually my first MM book was <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13570854.Lover_at_Last__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___11_" title="Lover at Last (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #11) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover at Last</a>. I was SO hooked! Then I read more MM and later I discovered I don't ever want to stop. Now I'd really want to stick to only MM.<br /><br />Back to this book. As I was saying: I really don't like fantasy or paranormal, but I grabbed this one because it was free on Amazon and I checked it on GR and saw all the high ratings for all the books in this series and so many of my friends loved it. <br />While scrolling through my MM books to read on my Kindle, something about the title and the cover made me open it. Well let me just tell you how sucked into the story I got. I kept reading and reading and I just couldn't put it down. This author's writing is very captivating to say the least! <br /><br /><b>Vampire Matthew is captured by incubus Tarrick. The General Tarrick reveals many things Matthew didn't even know about himself. There is a war between their kind and Matthew is forced to help those who kept him captive. But he falls desperately in love with Tarrick.</b> This would be all I can reveal, because what happens in this book should be discovered by every reader on his own. I hate spoilers and I'm glad I haven't stumbled upon any before starting it. <br /><br />What I loved here would be the uniqueness of the story, the flow and lightness of the reading, the suspense and also the unexpected hotness. Oh and there are SO many hot scenes! The incubi feed on sexual energy and they could also enchant others to fall for them or even do anything they want. Scary, right? <br /><br />What I really didn't like would be the ending. Tarrick disappointed me big time! Oh and all that sleeping around with females too put me off. It's not something I expected to find here. I was even considering giving it less stars, but I was too glued to the pages and awed by the unique world this author created. So I'm sticking with 4 stars.<br />We get a lot of fighting, blood, but also super hot scenes. I would have loved for Tarrick not to break Matthew's and my heart, but I hope he'll redeem himself in the next books. Off I go, jumping into the next one!</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2379674611?book_show_action=true">May 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2379674611" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11309451827815969184"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Not so bad, I guess*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br/>Usually my gut is right. Usually. However, deciding to go against my already decision to read the book wasn't really a mistake (as I had already shelved this book as a ‘checked won't read’ book). This is a first, I believe. First that I actually enjoyed - somewhat - after going back on my decision. Also, I thought this series was YA :O Boy was I wrong. The book centers around vampire <b>Matthew Callahan</b> (39, turns 40, though changed at 32) struggles with his nee</span>
  <span id="freeText11309451827815969184" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Not so bad, I guess*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br />Usually my gut is right. Usually. However, deciding to go against my already decision to read the book wasn't really a mistake (as I had already shelved this book as a ‘checked won't read’ book). This is a first, I believe. First that I actually enjoyed - somewhat - after going back on my decision. Also, I thought this series was YA :O Boy was I wrong. The book centers around vampire <b>Matthew Callahan</b> (39, turns 40, though changed at 32) struggles with his need to feed on humans. For seven years, he's been keeping to himself, all alone, until one night, he is lured into a trap and taken prisoner by High Lord <b>General Tarrick</b> (thousand-years-old) who is a seductive incubus who feeds off sexual energy. He is then forced to called Tarrick his ‘master’ and trained to become a weapon as Matthew is not only a vampire, he's also an incubus. This makes him dangerous, powerful and he can help stop the war between vampires and incubus'. Matthew is determent to get free, but first he needs to learn everything he can. <br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I have been fighting vampires for nearly a millennium. I have every possible means to kill a vampire at my disposal, but I have yet to decide which way your death would please me most.” A sinful smile crossed the man’s face and it was Matthew’s turn to be stunned. Just how old was he? Had he been fighting vampires for his entire life? If so, that placed him at nearly a thousand.<br />Suddenly thirty-nine didn’t seem so old. Matthew stopped aging the night he had been turned and wondered if other vampires counted their human years in their age. If not, he was seven. No wonder the man had been so shocked Matthew could break away from whatever he had been doing to him.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><b>Overall, I'm surprised that I actually liked it</b>. Sure, I didn't love it, far from it, but the plot was interesting and the characters had some potential. I like Matthew to a degree, but I still struggled with Tarrick. He is a cruel man, and <b>not in a hot way</b>, and I also found him weak as a person. Not my type :/ Story-wise, I liked that the timeline is for a period of time; months at least. However, the story was also predictable, and I wanted more from it. Also, I do hope that if there ever comes a time when Matthew gets together with for example Tarrick for real; like as a couple, <b>they will be monogamous</b>. I'm not all that into having multiple lovers. I more into ‘power couples’. On to the next one I guess.<br /> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>A slave to his hunger, he was still unable to sate his thirst. The first year had been terrible for him and he’d taken a life nearly every night.<br />All it took was for a human to pass too close to him and his world would melt into the wonderful fragrance of blood…the flow of it pumping through their veins…the thud of their heartbeat…<br />Whenever he’d hunted, Matthew would silently beg for his prey to escape, but they never got away from him. By the time a human realized what he was—and understood the danger they were in—it was too late.<br />They fought.<br />They screamed.<br />They begged.<br />They died.<br />And he loved it.<br />And he hated himself for loving it.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><b><u>Other characters</u>:</b><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<i>I've put these in a spoilers tag simply because it's a long list; contains spoilers</i><br />↦ <b>Silva</b> (sixty-three years old, though she looked as if she was in her mid-twenties), lieutenant. <br />↦ <b>Cullip</b>, commander. His team is called the Wardens. They're Tarrick’s personal bodyguards and the highest-ranking hunters currently at Ashwood. ‘Ashwood’ is both the estate and academy.<br />↦ <b>Lady Rosaline</b>, a succubi.<br />↦ <b>Emilia</b>, vampire with the rare ability to give humans nightmares while they sleep. <b>Stolus</b>, her defiant protector vampire. Both in cages by the incubus. Emilia and Stolus is Lord <b>Ascelina</b>'s kids.<br />↦ <b>High King Malarath</b>, has ruled longer than Tarrick been alive. There are other kings and queens all over the world but they all kneel to him. <br />↦ <b>Lillian ‘Lily’ Callahan </b>(18), as her father is incubus, she is then a succubus. Her mother, <b>Alyssa Callahan</b>, died two years ago because of a rare brain cancer. Lily is staying with <b>Lord Teleclus</b> (twenty-five hundred), a friend of Tarrick. He lives in a safe territory on the east coast that rarely sees vampires. He’s older than Tarrick, a retired Spartan warrior actually, but he’ll fight if he has to. He’s powerful and can protect her.<br />↦ <b>Lord Tane</b>, an incubus and Tarrick's son. <b>Tarquin</b>, Tarrick's eldest son. He was a general in his own right, favored to replace Tarrick should he ever fall. He had the near-impossible task of trying to fight the vampires in Russia. Tarrick has six children that still live; five males, one girl. <b>Talena ‘Lena’</b>, the daughter. Tarrick has lost eleven children as he raise warriors and it has been a long war.<br />↦ <b>Lady Dennith</b> (nearly eight hundred), an incubi and she is Tarrick's right hand. She fights as Tarrick's eyes and ears in battles and if he fall, she becomes the temporary High General until a new one is promoted. <br />↦ <b>Lord Vassu</b> (just over three hundred), an incubi and he is one of Tarrick's best warriors and usually fights in vampire territory. According to hunter gossip, he had recently gone through his third transformation. He had come out the other side of it as one of the biggest incubi around.<br />↦ <b>Fendrel</b>, the knight hunter as Matthew calls him, he's a special brand of hunter that specialized in taking down different monsters besides vampires: a dragon slayer. However, because dragons were sleeping and rarely woke, he was sent to join just about any fight happening. Some cadets had told Matthew that Fendrel was once a true knight during the middle ages, but Matthew was skeptical about that.<br />↦ <b>Hiroto of HouseKōki</b> (looked 18), commander and hunter. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[He's called a kitsune. A fox spirit. He's also older than Tarrick. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />↦ <b>Asper</b>, Tarrick’s gargoyle.<br />↦ <b>Queen Aglee</b>, the High King’s granddaughter, and her consort <b>Lord Ennius</b>, who was not a king but high ranked and respected all the same. Queen Agleea ruled most of the East Coast.<br />↦ <b>Priscilla</b>, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[daugther of Lord <b>Brodeur</b>, was held captured by the vampire for twenty-three years, one hundred and fifty-two days until Matthew saved her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />↦ <b>Prescott</b>, the High King’s commander and leader of the Argonauts—consisting of the six best hunters in the corps. Or so the trainees at Ashwood had told Matthew. He was inclined to believe them considering Imperator Prescott was one of the four people Matthew couldn’t compel without his collar blowing up.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He wanted to lick every one of Tarrick’s wounds to taste his blood and speed along the healing process. He wanted to place his bite marks on Tarrick’s neck. Fuck. Matthew wanted to ravage the incubus in every way possible. He wanted to fuck him and destroy him all at once.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br /><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Paranormal <s>Romance</s> (M/M of sorts).<br /><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book One.<br /><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>Favorite character?</b> - Matthew Callahan.<br /><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Sure, I guess.<br /><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Unsure.<br /><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - No. <br /><b>Rating</b> - 3 stars.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2305186740" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2989699997086477745"><br/>4.5*<br/><br/>Matthew Callahan is different. Seven years ago when he was thirty-two he was attacked and turned into a vampire. No that’s not why he’s different, there’s lots of vampires. There’s something else about him.<br/>He was attacked and left, he’s never known his sire. He’s had to figure things out on his own and he knows nothing about vampires despite being one for the past seven years.<br/><br/>One night he hears a thump.....and another and he can’t resist. He’s drawn to the sound, the feeling but it’s a trap </span>
  <span id="freeText2989699997086477745" style="display:none"><br />4.5*<br /><br />Matthew Callahan is different. Seven years ago when he was thirty-two he was attacked and turned into a vampire. No that’s not why he’s different, there’s lots of vampires. There’s something else about him.<br />He was attacked and left, he’s never known his sire. He’s had to figure things out on his own and he knows nothing about vampires despite being one for the past seven years.<br /><br />One night he hears a thump.....and another and he can’t resist. He’s drawn to the sound, the feeling but it’s a trap and Matthew finds himself captured by High Lord General Tarrick, a incubus.<br /><br />Despite the fact that he’s a prisoner he finds himself attracted to Tarrick. Matthews life as a vampire has been an incredibly lonely. He left his family to save them and he’s struggled on alone and so he craves love and companionship and more than anything he wants to belong.<br /><br />Tarrick uses him as a weapon against his own kind and Matthew does everything possible to him.<br /><br />This book is fabulous, it’s different and I found I couldn’t put it down, I was hooked and desperate to find out more about the mystery that is Matthew.<br /><br />It’s straight onto the next book Sire for me</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4943626967483299171">This book was beyond amazing, I was transported to another universe and I do not want to leave. It reminds me of the feeling I had when reading<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9305362.Captive_Prince__Captive_Prince___1_' title='Captive Prince (Captive Prince, #1) by C.S. Pacat' rel='nofollow noopener'>Captive Prince</a>, the character felt alive and I just wanted to know more about them. You'll think with a book with sucubbus, incubbus and vampires it would be a sex galore but it wasn't, sex played a part of it but did not completely overshadow it as it usually does with books like these. <br/><br/>My friend <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/69053579-shin-mon-thway' rel='nofollow noopener'>Shin</a> recommended this,this goes to show you how brilliant </span>
  <span id="freeText4943626967483299171" style="display:none">This book was beyond amazing, I was transported to another universe and I do not want to leave. It reminds me of the feeling I had when reading<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9305362.Captive_Prince__Captive_Prince___1_" title="Captive Prince (Captive Prince, #1) by C.S. Pacat" rel="nofollow noopener">Captive Prince</a>, the character felt alive and I just wanted to know more about them. You'll think with a book with sucubbus, incubbus and vampires it would be a sex galore but it wasn't, sex played a part of it but did not completely overshadow it as it usually does with books like these. <br /><br />My friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/69053579-shin-mon-thway" rel="nofollow noopener">Shin</a> recommended this,this goes to show you how brilliant she is because this is earning a spot amongst my favs.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1838430025" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer328664219878015291"><b><i>Well, well, well...</i><br/><br/>This turned out to be a tasty little morsel.</b> <br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/31359082.Captive__Beautiful_Monsters__1_' title='Captive (Beautiful Monsters #1) by Jex Lane' rel='nofollow noopener'>Captive</a> is an urban fantasy that's a little bit enemies to lovers and a whole lot bad wrong. Matthew is a vampire/incubus hybrid without a sire out hunting one night when he feels a "thump". Said "thump" is not Thumper but Tarrick, general baddie, sex king and ancient incubus general. Drawn like a tractor beam to him, his first sexual attraction to a man in case you were wondering and WHOOPSIE! Matthew finds himself in a pickle. How</span>
  <span id="freeText328664219878015291" style="display:none"><b><i>Well, well, well...</i><br /><br />This turned out to be a tasty little morsel.</b> <br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/31359082.Captive__Beautiful_Monsters__1_" title="Captive (Beautiful Monsters #1) by Jex Lane" rel="nofollow noopener">Captive</a> is an urban fantasy that's a little bit enemies to lovers and a whole lot bad wrong. Matthew is a vampire/incubus hybrid without a sire out hunting one night when he feels a "thump". Said "thump" is not Thumper but Tarrick, general baddie, sex king and ancient incubus general. Drawn like a tractor beam to him, his first sexual attraction to a man in case you were wondering and WHOOPSIE! Matthew finds himself in a pickle. However, for one so young he is exceedingly powerful which is precisely what gets him out of said pickle with Tarrick and his hunter/incubi entourage.<br /><br />Well, sort of gets him out of a pickle. It gets him not dead so that's a win, but then the bad wrong begins. Suffice to say, these two paranormal superpowers do not see eye to eye and have been at war for centuries so... what's a little torture of a young vamp?<br /><br />To be clear, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/31359082.Captive__Beautiful_Monsters__1_" title="Captive (Beautiful Monsters #1) by Jex Lane" rel="nofollow noopener">Captive</a> is not torture porn but it is certainly violent and dark. Yet, despite, or maybe because of, all the bad wrong there is definitely <i>something</i> between Matthew and Tarrick. I'm just not sure what that something is at this point which is part of what intrigues me about this series.<br /><br />The other selling point is the action. What can I say? I'm feeling a little bloodthirsty. There is action galore! It was glorious: fighting, decapitation, slaughter, destruction, bludgeoning and general savagery abound. There are some unusual paranormal beings and a fair amount of sexy times happening too. <b>WARNING: all of these characters are bisexual thus there is m/f sex on page.</b><br /><br />All of the above in and of itself would be persuasive enough reasons to read this story but what takes it next level is Lane's crafting of these characters as not just morally grey but complex and layered, not just the main characters either. There are many, many characters all of which are pulling their weight in this story. That's rare imo. Many of them oftentimes make unexpected and/or infuriating decisions but that is precisely what makes this story so riveting and difficult to put down. <br /><br />So, apologies to my review books. I'll get to you. One day.<br /><br />If any of the above looks like your kind of thing, you will likely lose a few days to this series. I know I'm about to.</span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText1914573507810036636" style="display:none">3.5*<br />Monsters? yes. Beautiful? I don’t think so.<br />I’m still not sure whether I liked this book or not? Vampires fight against Incubi and vice versa. Matthew, the hero who tells us this story, is a mongrel. A Vampire Incubus hybrid. And it is as it is imagined. Vampires bite, drink blood, kill, burn in the light, tolerate no silver, and the older they become the more powerful they are. They develop special skills and can fly. And they can impose their will on others.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480230708i/21286830._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story was really exciting. Especially the beginning and the end have wrapped me around the finger. The battle scenes should not have been so extended to my taste. I don't like mass-fighting scenes. Even if these are well-written. But it is war and how should the author otherwise show us Matthew's skills in progress.<br>Right!<br><s>The only thing that keeps me from reading the next one in this series: part 2 ends with a cliffhanger. Therefore, I will wait until part 3 is released. Early in 2017.</s><br>Uhm ... Scratch that ... Can not wait. So it goes on!<br><br>That is annoying.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480230708i/21286831._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For now, Matthew is free.<br>And by the way ... I don't believe Tarrick a single word!<br><br><i>“Who were you eavesdropping on?” <br>“No one,” Matthew said and slipped out of his tuxedo jacket, setting it on the railing. <br>“You should learn to lie better.” <br>“I don’t answer to…” Matthew stopped speaking when he noticed Hiroto’s shadow. The lights at the door had Hiroto backlit, his shadow—upside down from Matthew’s perspective—was that of a small four-legged creature. It had pointed ears and bushy tails. Many bushy tails. Matthew stood and walked beside Hiroto to look at the shadow upright. It was a fox. “Holy shit, you aren’t human.” <br>A sly smile crossed Hiroto’s face. “Never said I was.” <br>“I thought all hunters were human.” <br>“Nope.”</i><br><br>The side characters were beautifully drawn. And I really hope to read more from the little fox!<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <br>
  <i>“You are too powerful, too clever, to be allowed to continue with the amount of freedom you have been shown so far.” <br>“What…?” Matthew said. He hardly had any freedoms. <br>Tarrick continued, ignoring Matthew. “You are being transferred to another facility where you will be kept caged except during training or when ordered to a battle.” <br>“No…” He was going to be caged again. Alone. Anger rose within him.“I came back…” <br>“I know you did, Matthew.” <br>Matthew balled his hands into fists. “I was offered everything and I came back.” <br>“I know.” <br>“I am loyal.” <br>“Not everyone is convinced that you are.” <br>“Please…don’t let them lock me up alone. I’m an incubus. I don’t want to be alone again. I need to be with my people.” <br>“You will be moved to New York tomorrow night.” <br>“I want to stay with you. I…” Matthew loved him but the words stuck in his throat. He was too scared. <br>“You don’t love me,” Tarrick said it for him. <br>“I do,” Matthew whispered.<br>“You don’t. It was all manufactured to control you.” <br>Matthew stared at him. “No. That’s not true. I know how I feel.” <br>Tarrick’s face betrayed nothing. “Incubi are masters of manipulating emotion, you know this, and I have been breaking vampires since I was young. I am exceedingly skilled in doing so. None of it was real.”<br></i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7835308912752804480">2.5 stars<br/><br/>One of those weird books where I was glued and it was so, so hard to put down (kept me up too late last night), but I was disgusted and angered most of the time. It left me feeling frustrated. I almost bought the sequel but I peeked ahead at the reviews to see if it gets better - it doesn't (the situation), so I'll pass. I don't mind dark stuff, but I hate piss-me-off, unfair stuff.<br/><br/>I liked Matthew, although he was clearly a monster of sorts, but I root for the underdog, the oppressed, t</span>
  <span id="freeText7835308912752804480" style="display:none">2.5 stars<br /><br />One of those weird books where I was glued and it was so, so hard to put down (kept me up too late last night), but I was disgusted and angered most of the time. It left me feeling frustrated. I almost bought the sequel but I peeked ahead at the reviews to see if it gets better - it doesn't (the situation), so I'll pass. I don't mind dark stuff, but I hate piss-me-off, unfair stuff.<br /><br />I liked Matthew, although he was clearly a monster of sorts, but I root for the underdog, the oppressed, the abused. I look for redemption and them being able to raise up. Matthew was abused, abandoned, ignored, abused, beaten, abused, used, abused, not appreciated, abused and finally - spit in the face at the end. I couldn't stand the incubus, I really couldn't. What was so maddening is even though they clearly didn't deserve his loyalty anymore, he still kept trying, much like the vulnerable and abused tend to. Forced captivity pisses me off too - I would have been plotting the death of the whole house.<br /><br />Matthew was too wishy washy too. He kept changing his mind and bending way too easy under his abuser's influence when it came to leaving. I know he wanted to belong somewhere but you should only give so many chances before you flip the proverbial bird and sail off into the sunset.<br /><br />I did like the uniqueness of his abilities, the worldbuilding, and the writing style overall. Tarrick mainly pissed me off (can't stand him), and it's hard to invest in relationships since he freely slept with so many anyway. It just didn't feel like actual chemistry or anything special to me - if anything, I'd rather them remain total enemies.<br /><br />I'm curious on the other books, but this one already gave me too much reader rage to continue. I did like the ending, though. Take that!</span>

<div id="review_1730975743" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1730975743" />
    <a title="Jo * Smut-Dickted *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3389302-jo-smut-dickted"><img alt="Jo * Smut-Dickted *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1511535164p2/3389302.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1730975743?book_show_action=true">Aug 17, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo * Smut-Dickted *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo * Smut-Dickted *" href="/user/show/3389302-jo-smut-dickted">Jo * Smut-Dickted *</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780997753301" href="/book/show/30955295-captive">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3389302-jo-smut-dickted?shelf=read-on-kindle">read-on-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3389302-jo-smut-dickted?shelf=theme-capture-dubcon-slave">theme-capture-dubcon-slave</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3389302-jo-smut-dickted?shelf=sex-pairing-mf">sex-pairing-mf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3389302-jo-smut-dickted?shelf=paranormal-vampires">paranormal-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3389302-jo-smut-dickted?shelf=2019-sh-recs">2019-sh-recs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3389302-jo-smut-dickted?shelf=m-m-romance">m-m-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3389302-jo-smut-dickted?shelf=paranormal-incubus">paranormal-incubus</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3389302-jo-smut-dickted?shelf=theme-dark-oh-so-dark">theme-dark-oh-so-dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3389302-jo-smut-dickted?shelf=paranormal-general">paranormal-general</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1730975743" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16781264621047575298">I waver on 4 vs 5 stars. This book is <i> exactly</i> the type of book I love. Torture porn is good with me - though this isn't it frankly. My torture porn is way grittier and way darker. This had darkness but overall it's not really that dark (JMHO) except in theme. There is a strong redemption theme threading here - mixed in w/love, community, family. It's an intoxicating combo. The mindfuckery alone here is so very worthy of your time - is it real or Memorex? The fifth star was earned the last 10%. </span>
  <span id="freeText16781264621047575298" style="display:none">I waver on 4 vs 5 stars. This book is <i> exactly</i> the type of book I love. Torture porn is good with me - though this isn't it frankly. My torture porn is way grittier and way darker. This had darkness but overall it's not really that dark (JMHO) except in theme. There is a strong redemption theme threading here - mixed in w/love, community, family. It's an intoxicating combo. The mindfuckery alone here is so very worthy of your time - is it real or Memorex? The fifth star was earned the last 10%. Things got all real up in there...and I was relishing it completely. <br /><br />The world building is intriguing - but there were times I could not tell if I was in a castle ala 1600's or in a modern world setting. I know it's the latter but elements of the former permeated the story. Made it a bit harder to think of in my head. <br /><br />It's not a romance - and that's actually the main issue. It <b> feels</b> like it wants to be a romance. Like it's tipping into romancelandia and then it pulls itself back - sometimes artificially. Matthew is <b> not</b> a good guy. He's a vampire that preys on humans. Whether he wants to or not - he does it. Some of them, maybe many of them, are innocent. This ain't Dexter. He's a guy who does bad things. To live yes...however if he was as altruistic as we are constantly told he is then he would have walked into the sunrise long, long ago. His perfection makes him more of a romance MC than a general fiction MC. That eroded the star rating for some of the book. It's not until the last 15% that the tide changed - and I started to really "see" the real world parallels so clearly - oddly enough that made vampires and incubi seem human. <br /><br />I liked Tarrick quite a lot and he didn't really change natures. He also does bad things, a victim and a victor of the world he lives in, and containing light and dark (though..lotsa dark, lotsa jaded, lotsa mindfuckery). These two are the MC's in a non-romance romance. I actually didn't find the sex too hot - could have been a lot hotter (though there was one scene that was smokin') but it's not a focus and it felt so so. Admittedly I don't like consensual MF so that affected my enjoyment. YMMV here. I feel like there needed to be more sex focus - after all they are incubi and feed from sexual energy - raw, gritty, harsh, unrepentant -- that's what I wanted and it peeks through here like a rainbow but vanishes just as quick. <br /><br />The thing the thing...is "The" way, to everyone else, Matthew was perfect and un-killable. But Tarrick can take him down anytime. Physical? Mental? What? Really? A major disconnect and dissonance for me while reading. Matthew's very utter perfection grated on me and made me scrunch my face up while reading oh so many times. I wasn't feeling it and feeling him until way far in --- on a deeper level. <br /><br />I liked some of the secondary characters - and the violence was yummy in that oh so taboo way. The total disregard for human life never got any play time - and that could have had more exploration to really cement that these two guys and this world are not any form of Utopia. So it felt a very little like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9305362.Captive_Prince__Captive_Prince___1_" title="Captive Prince (Captive Prince, #1) by C.S. Pacat" rel="nofollow noopener">Captive Prince</a> but w/o the nuances and the sexual tension - and the right/wrong being gray/black/white at the same time. I very much enjoyed it - and am looking forward to the next one. <br /><br />And, frankly, I only write any sort of critical review and give it 5 stars still if I see so much promise and potential - so that gives you an indication of how much I did like this despite it's shortcomings. An author to watch!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16781264621047575298" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1838483419" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15696705752290570248">4 Stars<br/><br/>Excellent story and I love the Incubus vs. Vampire story-line.<br/><br/>Would have been closer to 5 stars if not for the pages and pages of graphic MF sex in a book purported to be an MM romance. I didn't bother to count but I think there were more, and more graphic, MF scenes than there were MM scenes. Yeah, not interested...so after that first one with Tarrick and the two succubi I skimmed the rest. (Two more long, descriptive scenes with Matthew and another succubus.)<br/><br/>I mean, I get it; incubi/suc</span>
  <span id="freeText15696705752290570248" style="display:none">4 Stars<br /><br />Excellent story and I love the Incubus vs. Vampire story-line.<br /><br />Would have been closer to 5 stars if not for the pages and pages of graphic MF sex in a book purported to be an MM romance. I didn't bother to count but I think there were more, and more graphic, MF scenes than there were MM scenes. Yeah, not interested...so after that first one with Tarrick and the two succubi I skimmed the rest. (Two more long, descriptive scenes with Matthew and another succubus.)<br /><br />I mean, I get it; incubi/succubi are creatures of sex and need/take it from anyone regardless of gender. I just didn't appreciate that we were shorted on the scenes with Tarrick &amp; Matthew. IMHO, it would have made Matthew's attraction and dedication to Tarrick more believable and his heart-ache more understandable if we'd gotten more of them as a couple in order to feel that emotion. Instead, the emotional turmoil and sense of betrayal at the end feels scripted, forced...like we're being <i>told</i> this is how he feels instead of being able to see it. (I skimmed bits of the Matthew/Rosaline scene but even only reading snatches here and there it felt like they had more of a connection than Matthew did with Tarrick, so that imbalance really did the story an injustice.)<br /><br />I'll still put the sequel on the TBR because the entire arc is interesting. (Sentient Gargoyles FTW!!) I'd like to find out who Matthew's parents are, and who sired him. Also, what started the war and why it's ongoing. Maybe even how the shifters have almost been wiped out. And while part of me thinks that Tarrick's actions were a kindness to sever ties and allow Matthew to move on, the way the book is written really makes that questionable; if he actually did manipulate Matthew like that then I totally want Matthew to get some righteous revenge on that fucker.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15696705752290570248" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I just got Kindle Unlimited, and I've been availing myself of <i>all </i>the dark romance my smutty heart desires, and this was one of the romances that's been at the top of my list for a while. Incubi and vampires have been at war for a while, but now Matthew, a man who previously believed himself to be an ordinary vampire, is a key player in the sinister machinations of the incubus and succubus army.<br><br><br><br>Tarrick is a lord general in the incubi army, and Matthew's captor. It kind of fell apart, though, since there are lots of dull scenes interspersed with some pretty abusive sex. I'm not one to shy away from toxic romances but it has to work. I would probably rate this higher if I forced myself through it but at the moment, I can't be bothered, and if a book isn't good enough to see to the end, that's on the book.<br><br><br><br>1.5 stars</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2760894540506260544"><b>4.5 Stars!</b><br/><br/>Wow. Not sure what else to say. <br/><br/>This one must've hit my feed. The blurb sounded interesting and the series as a whole has pretty high reviews. <br/><br/>I don't read a lot of paranormal, not that I don't enjoy it. <br/><br/>I found this one really interesting. Not to mention intriguing and exciting. The fighting scenes. The whole incubi feeding off of sex thing. The world building. The storyline. The different beings. <br/>All of it. <br/><br/>Consider me hooked.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8529604809383590096"><br/>Mm.<br/><br/>Well, I finished it. <br/><br/>This book started off as a 5 star, then went down to 3 because of how boring and flat it was in the middle, and ended on a solid 4 star.<br/><br/>To say that this book was a romance novel, was kiiiiinda a stretch since both the main characters Matthew and Tarrick are sucking, licking, kissing, tasting and fucking someone else every now and then. On top of that, despite Matthew's moaning about how he has fallen for Tarrick and how he only lives for Tarricks glorious gigantic magnifi</span>
  <span id="freeText8529604809383590096" style="display:none"><br>Mm.<br><br>Well, I finished it. <br><br>This book started off as a 5 star, then went down to 3 because of how boring and flat it was in the middle, and ended on a solid 4 star.<br><br>To say that this book was a romance novel, was kiiiiinda a stretch since both the main characters Matthew and Tarrick are sucking, licking, kissing, tasting and fucking someone else every now and then. On top of that, despite Matthew's moaning about how he has fallen for Tarrick and how he only lives for Tarricks glorious gigantic magnificent dick, I still can't really feel the connection between the two. There's barely any chemistry whatsoever other than the constant need to fuck, so Matthew's feeling for his "Master" seems a tad too rushed.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1568671412ra/28157693.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>Another thing, like some of the reviewers here mentioned, this book did a <i>whole</i> lot of telling and not enough showing. There was a shit ton of: <br><br><i>He was brushing his teeth, and then he went to shower. But not before he remembered that he wanted oh.so.fucking.badly to fuck Tarrick. He loved the way Tarrick and his purple/blue/green whatever eyes, fucked. At first Tarrick would hold his hips down and then bla blabla bla bla</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1571093240ra/28293984.gif" width="450" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>It was good that this book was written in simple and easy to understand words, cause if the author tried to be flowery and shit with her words with all the constant description that she shoved down our throats, I would have thrown up words. And then DNF-ed.<br><br>Oh not to mention, too much sex. Not enough content. I get that this is the world of incubi and whatnot, but I mean, since it's a novel first and foremost, I would really work on developing the characters more, rather than just constantly making my characters having sex all the fucking damn time. But hey, that's just me. <br><br>Other than that, no real complaints. Book was addicting, which made it easy to want to keep reading. For now, I am curious enough to continue to book 2 and see how things unfold. <br><br><br><br><b> Blog : <a href="http://literaturesandmovies.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Click here for more of my reviews</a><br><br><br></b></span>

<div id="review_1702703802" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1702703802" />
    <a title="Kristen Burns" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/42225826-kristen-burns"><img alt="Kristen Burns" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1436601871p2/42225826.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1702703802?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristen Burns" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristen Burns" href="/user/show/42225826-kristen-burns">Kristen Burns</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=review-copy">review-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=read-2016-books">read-2016-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=paranormal-urban-fantasy">paranormal-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=fave-male-character">fave-male-character</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42225826-kristen-burns?shelf=incubi-succubi">incubi-succubi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1702703802" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16914042894945638847"><b>4 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Full Review:</b><br/>*I received a free ecopy of this book from the author in exchange for an honest review.*<br/><br/>If you like sex and violence, <i>man, is this ever the book for you!</i><br/><br/>This book is <i>full</i> of sex and violence. But it's also full vampires and incubi, twists and turns, and all sorts of good stuff.<br/><br/>I was immediately drawn in by the writing style because it was simple, but Matthew's voice came through really well and just clicked with me. <i>He</i> just clicked with me, actually. I didn't necessarily relat</span>
  <span id="freeText16914042894945638847" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Full Review:</b><br />*I received a free ecopy of this book from the author in exchange for an honest review.*<br /><br />If you like sex and violence, <i>man, is this ever the book for you!</i><br /><br />This book is <i>full</i> of sex and violence. But it's also full vampires and incubi, twists and turns, and all sorts of good stuff.<br /><br />I was immediately drawn in by the writing style because it was simple, but Matthew's voice came through really well and just clicked with me. <i>He</i> just clicked with me, actually. I didn't necessarily relate to him, but he was interesting with emotions that made me feel for him and a sense of humor that I loved.<br /><br />The dynamic between Matthew and Tarrick was interesting right off the bat as well, and I couldn't wait to see where that would go. I ended up disliking Tarrick for how manipulative and cruel he could be, but that's not a negative issue with the book, just my feelings about him as a character.<br /><br />The book was then made even better by this really amazing twist partway through that I just LOVED.<br /><br />There was also a vampire-incubus war that encompassed the plot since Tarrick was a general for the incubi, but, thankfully, the book always stayed focused on Matthew and his part in things. And I ended up finding the incubi society and military interesting. I felt so conflicted throughout the story though! Even I didn't know which side Matthew would be better off with, which one was less monstrous, or whom he should trust, so I could only imagine how hard it was for <i>him</i> to figure it out. And then that ending threw me for a loop since it was both terrible and amazing for Matthew.<br /><br />But between the war, Matthew's inner beast that reveled in the killing and bloodshed, and Matthew constantly getting beat or tortured in some way or other, there was, as I said, A LOT of violence. Not a bad thing, just a warning to anyone who doesn't (or does) like that.<br /><br />Also as I said, there was also a lot of sex, both M/M and M/F, though unfortunately not a lot of sex + blood drinking. The vampires were a nice blend of sexy and predatory, but it seemed like they were more on the predatory side (or maybe we just haven't gotten to the sexy blood drinking yet in the series).<br /><br />Last but not least, I can't not mention that there were also some kickass, terrifying gargoyles!<br /><br />The only negative thing I can say is that master/slave romance generally isn't my thing. (Not that this was a romance, but there were feelings and sex, so close enough.) I just don't find it believable that a slave would be attracted to or fall in love with his master. Vampires and incubi, however, just so happen to be my two favorite paranormal creatures, so there was no way I could resist this book. And you know what? Matthew did feel broken when he was eventually forced to submit, plus he felt super conflicted and confused by his feelings, so this was actually one of the more palatable portrayals I've read. Mostly though, this book just ended up being so good that I didn't even care if that aspect wasn't entirely believable.<br /><br />So overall, this book was basically 300-something pages of sex and violence, but a well-written 300-something pages of sex and violence with a twisty story behind it, a great main character, and an interesting incubus society!<br /><br /><b>Recommended For:</b><br />Anyone who likes vampires, incubi, sex, and violence. Anyone who likes master/slave romance (romance being used loosely as it's mostly just sex).<br /><br /><b>
  <a href="http://wp.me/p6ovgw-1JQ" rel="nofollow noopener">Original Review @ Metaphors and Moonlight</a>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="16914042894945638847" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1754853237" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1754853237" />
    <a title="Tatiana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43237592-tatiana"><img alt="Tatiana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485239594p2/43237592.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1754853237?book_show_action=true">Sep 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tatiana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tatiana" href="/user/show/43237592-tatiana">Tatiana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780997753301" href="/book/show/30955295-captive">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43237592-tatiana?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1754853237" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3719027519196034438">The good parts are that the paranormal aspect of this book is pretty interesting (if you're able of throwing all your logic out of the window) and it's a fast-paced read with quite a bit of sex, gore and violence.<br/><br/>All the rest is extremely disappointing.<br/><br/>- The writing style is really simple, and it's all “tell” and no “show" to boot. I like my books to be a little more on the sophisticated side.<br/><br/>- The main characters' personalities are practically non-existent, almost like they're just cardboard cu</span>
  <span id="freeText3719027519196034438" style="display:none">The good parts are that the paranormal aspect of this book is pretty interesting (if you're able of throwing all your logic out of the window) and it's a fast-paced read with quite a bit of sex, gore and violence.<br /><br />All the rest is extremely disappointing.<br /><br />- The writing style is really simple, and it's all “tell” and no “show" to boot. I like my books to be a little more on the sophisticated side.<br /><br />- The main characters' personalities are practically non-existent, almost like they're just cardboard cutouts. <br /><br />- The humans here are nothing more than food and cannon fodder, and all the characters are basically monsters with little to no moral qualms about killing, so it's hard to feel any sympathy for them. <br /><br />- This is <b>NOT</b> a romance book, it's an erotic urban fantasy. The only "romantic" part here is when Matthew admits that he's falling for Tarrick but that doesn't actually stop him from having sex with other people. And Tarrick doesn't seem to give a flying fuck about Matthew. <br />Hopefully the next book will have more romance, but I highly doubt it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3719027519196034438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2060297363" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2060297363" />
    <a title="Meagan ✊&amp;#x1f3fc; Blacklivesmatter ✊&amp;#x1f3fc;Blacktranslivesmatter" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27847867-meagan-x1f3fc-blacklivesmatter-x1f3fc-blacktranslivesmatter"><img alt="Meagan ✊&amp;#x1f3fc; Blacklivesmatter ✊&amp;#x1f3fc;Blacktranslivesmatter" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572058255p2/27847867.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2060297363?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Meagan ✊&amp;#x1f3fc; Blacklivesmatter ✊&amp;#x1f3fc;Blacktranslivesmatter" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Meagan ✊&amp;#x1f3fc; Blacklivesmatter ✊&amp;#x1f3fc;Blacktranslivesmatter" href="/user/show/27847867-meagan-x1f3fc-blacklivesmatter-x1f3fc-blacktranslivesmatter">Meagan ✊&amp;#x1f3fc; Blacklivesmatter ✊&amp;#x1f3fc;Blacktranslivesmatter</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27847867-meagan-x1f3fc-blacklivesmatter-x1f3fc-blacktranslivesmatter?shelf=dark-taboo-romance">dark-taboo-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27847867-meagan-x1f3fc-blacklivesmatter-x1f3fc-blacktranslivesmatter?shelf=lgbtqia">lgbtqia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27847867-meagan-x1f3fc-blacklivesmatter-x1f3fc-blacktranslivesmatter?shelf=pnr-sci-fi-romance-smut">pnr-sci-fi-romance-smut</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27847867-meagan-x1f3fc-blacklivesmatter-x1f3fc-blacktranslivesmatter?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27847867-meagan-x1f3fc-blacklivesmatter-x1f3fc-blacktranslivesmatter?shelf=homonormative-societies">homonormative-societies</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2060297363" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1301698022842187010">I was absolutely in love with this story from beginning to end! I already love a good vampire story, but add all the unique elements and this story was taken to the next level. It was so refreshing. And I loved Matthew! <br/><br/>The world building:<br/>We get to see some unique and interesting twists on all the standard vampire tropes. We also see appearances by other supernatural creatures (Gargoyles, kitsune, shifters, Incubi and Succubi). However the focus was on Matthew, the vampire, and Tarrick, the Incu</span>
  <span id="freeText1301698022842187010" style="display:none">I was absolutely in love with this story from beginning to end! I already love a good vampire story, but add all the unique elements and this story was taken to the next level. It was so refreshing. And I loved Matthew! <br /><br />The world building:<br />We get to see some unique and interesting twists on all the standard vampire tropes. We also see appearances by other supernatural creatures (Gargoyles, kitsune, shifters, Incubi and Succubi). However the focus was on Matthew, the vampire, and Tarrick, the Incubus. The Incubi/Succubi society/culture was interesting. The thing that really stood out was that there was so much sexual fluidity. No one cared who slept with who (no slut shaming and no homophobia). I LOVED IT! Lane incorporating the Incubi/Succubi into the story was a brilliant idea. It opened the world up to so many possibilities. <br /><br />The characters:<br /><br />Matthew:<br />We are introduced to Matthew just a mere seven years after he has become a vampire. He has adjusted to his fate, but everything changes when he meets Tarrick, who takes him captive. Matthew knows nothing of the supernatural world that exists beyond vampires. He barely knows anything about what it truly means to be a vampire. While in captivity in the Incubi/Succubi society, he begins to discover many hidden abilities. This was one of the most interesting aspects of the book! <br /><br />I loved Matthew! 😍😍 He was so naive and kind hearted. Of course, Tarrick took advantage of that in every way possible. I hated to see Matthew held in captivity and I seriously hope he gets his revenge! 😈😈 His character had so many interesting layers. <br /><br />Tarrick:<br />I HATE HIM! I could have forgiven him at one point, but by the end I knew I never could. There was not one moment in this story where I wanted Matthew and Tarrick to actually be together romantically. But, oh boy, did I enjoy their page time together!!!<br /><br />Another character I loved was Rosaline. She was such a sweet heart to Matthew! I also liked Hiroto. I hope he makes an appearance in the next book! I pretty much loved anybody who helped Matthew and didn't use him or make his captivity worse. <br /><br />The plot and pacing:<br />This story is set against the backdrop of a war spanning millennia. So we do get some awesome action/battle scenes. We get see Matthew steadily transforming and learning new abilities. The pacing was perfect. I was immediately sucked in to Matthew's story. Things were constantly happening, but we also got a well fleshed out story and characters. <br /><br />Overall I loved it and can't wait to continue this series!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1301698022842187010" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Ok, let's begin with Matthew, our MC. He has been a vampire for seven years but his sire abandoned him after he had turned him so he is kind of lost in his new life.   <span id="freeText8136906378351703796" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>'vampires &amp; incubi'</i> stars</b><br /><br />This book was wonderful and I loved it so very much I don't even know where to start. Ok, let's begin with Matthew, our MC. He has been a vampire for seven years but his sire abandoned him after he had turned him so he is kind of lost in his new life. He doesn't really know much about what exactly means to be a vampire. For instance, he has no idea that he can compel someone or that he can hide from the sun in the earth (that's quite gross btw). And most important he doesn't know that his race is in a war with incubi and has been for centuries. Actually millenniums more likely. So when he stumbles across an incubus it doesn't occur to him that he should run and hide. And that he definitely should not try to eat him.<br /><br />Of course, this incubus is not just some random harmless demon, he is High Lord General Tarrick who's been killing vampires for about seven or eight hundred years. But Tarrick discovers another thing about Matthew that he hasn't been aware of - he is not only a vampire but an incubus as well. So instead of killing him, Tarrick takes him for a slave. My poor Matthew. He was abandoned first by his incubi parents and then by his vampire sire too. He is like some kind of a lost little puppy who wouldn't hurt a fly (well, he is killing humans by feeding on them but let's not dwell on this for too long). Anyway, he is such an amazing character. He is only trying to survive in a world that he does not even completely understand and everyone around is treating him really badly. These incubi are just a bunch of hypocrites. All of them who are hurting my Matthew are on my shit list. Starting with Tarrick. <br /><br />Well, in truth, I can't really make my mind about him. Yes, I'm seriously mad at him because of everything he's done to Matthew but he is a great character too. And oh so hot which is a little strange since incubi are quite monstrous in their true form. Claws, horns, wings, tail, hooves, yes, you heard that right, fucking hooves (I'm trying to forget that part as it reminds me too much of o pony-play and that's something I don't find sexy at all.) I was trying to say that I could have liked Tarrick as I like Matthew if he would only stop being such an idiot. He is this gorgeous warrior Viking born incubus who is such a badass but in reality, he is no better than a slave himself. I understand he's been a soldier for so long that obeying commands is probably in his blood. But for fuck sake, if his balls are as impressive as his dick then he better finds them real quick and tells the High King to go fuck himself. I hope he gets what he deserves for what he did to Matthew. I don't want something horrible for him but some penance would do him good. And I still haven't decided if I want Matthew and Tarrick to be together. They sure are hot together and I think that Tarrick lied about these cruel things he said to him. I want for Matthew to be happy and with someone who deserves him. If only Tarrick would man up. Well, we'll see in the next book.<br /><br />There're also so many other fabulous characters. Lady Rosaline who I hated at first but she is actually really sweet. And I'm very intrigued by Hiroto. He is so cute and I'm pretty sure he is kinky little foxy. Must be these fluffy ears. I don't know yet what to think about Ascelina. Good or bad, she is interesting. And can someone please kill lord Tane. Matthew felt as if he had conquered all of Rome.<br /><br />Oh shit. Matthew couldn’t believe Tane just said that. He wanted to be anywhere else but here right now. Even the underground prison was starting to sound good.<br /><br />“I know my position might seem harsh, but always remember that even I have people I kneel before and must give my allegiance to. Collar or no, we all have our masters.”<br />One day, that would be different for Matthew. One day, others would kneel before him.</i><br /><br />My original almost review<br />Holy shit, that was fuckintastic!!!! I loved it, loved it, loved it. RTC when I come to my senses LOL</span>

<div id="review_3463704919" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3463704919" />
    <a title="M.I.A" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/106686359-m-i-a"><img alt="M.I.A" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585443555p2/106686359.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3463704919?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="M.I.A" class="user" itemprop="url" name="M.I.A" href="/user/show/106686359-m-i-a">M.I.A</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/106686359-m-i-a?shelf=paranormal-misc-mixed">paranormal-misc-mixed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/106686359-m-i-a?shelf=steam-high-or-erotica">steam-high-or-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/106686359-m-i-a?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/106686359-m-i-a?shelf=lgbtq-fiction">lgbtq-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/106686359-m-i-a?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3463704919" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12802096239403288234">This series has been incredibly <b>engrossing and addictive</b>. I could not put it down and binge read all three full-length books back to back. <br/><br/>At first it was a bit jarring being thrown into the world of Vampires and Incubus’s without much back story. But at about 20-30% everything began to flow seamlessly and it only get's more intense as the series goes on. <br/><br/>This paranormal world rampant with <b>war, grudges, politics, violence, betrayals, manipulation, sex … </b><br/>It’s a dark world where violence is part o</span>
  <span id="freeText12802096239403288234" style="display:none">This series has been incredibly <b>engrossing and addictive</b>. I could not put it down and binge read all three full-length books back to back. <br /><br />At first it was a bit jarring being thrown into the world of Vampires and Incubus’s without much back story. But at about 20-30% everything began to flow seamlessly and it only get's more intense as the series goes on. <br /><br />This paranormal world rampant with <b>war, grudges, politics, violence, betrayals, manipulation, sex … </b><br />It’s a dark world where violence is part of the norm. <br />Where Incubus’s and Vampires despise one another and have been killing each other for as long as they could remember. <br />An alternate world where the supernatural exist hidden from human eyes. <br /><b>Creatures</b> the likes of dragons, fairies, shifters, witches, demons, gods, gargoyles, oracles, mermaids… <br /><br /><b>The Incubus’s</b> were the most unexpected entity of all. Yes, they gain sustenance through sexual energy but the cool part is they’re not just sex symbols, some are fearsome warriors and they have terrifying incubus aspects that’s more in the lane of ‘demon’ form, horns, tails and all. <br /><br />Above all else this is <b>Matthew Callahan’s story</b>. Once upon a time a fireman, father, husband only to lose his entire identity when he’s turned and abandoned as a Vampire. Without a sire, fearful of his very nature and very alone in unwelcoming and unknown world. <br /><b>Matthew</b> who becomes reluctantly caught up in the on going war between the Incubus’s and Vampires. <br /><b>Matthew</b> who will be <b>broken, destroyed, betrayed, manipulated, debased, tortured, desired, feared, loved, despised…</b> You name it, he goes through it, and just when you think it couldn’t possibly be worse, it will be. <br />Despite it all, Matthew retains this hopefulness. His desperate need to belong somewhere, anywhere. To love and be loved in return. His ability to forgive, to discard his own pain. He’s the kind of character that pulls at your heart strings, that makes you ache for him, that brings you to tears. <br /><br />Don’t expect a conventional <b>love story</b> because circumstances simply don’t allow such a thing. Incubus’s for one are notorious for their varied sexual partners so monogamy is out. There is also a vicious war going on during all three books, a bit distracting. But that doesn’t mean there aren’t certain emotions. Even <b>forbidden love</b> at play here. <br />Many captivating characters will make themselves known but it’s worth discovering without me spoiling it. But one character reveals himself early enough he’s worth a mention. <br /><br /><b>Tarrick.</b> Charming and cruel High Lord General of the Incubus’s. High up and the food chain, feared and respected by all. I wish I could have gotten inside his head. He’s one of those characters that’s multiple steps ahead of everyone else. His motivations always unclear. His manipulation game unmatched. Even after all three books I’m still not quite certain Tarrick can ever truly redeem himself, but even at his cruelest there is something about him. Minute glimmers of humanity, tenderness that somehow give you hope. His carefully controlled un-emotional mask quivering just a tiny bit. Tarrick is a warrior, commanding, intelligent, fearsome, vicious, controlled and the second he shows any glimmer of something real he becomes irresistible. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>This is a captivating and addictive series. Highly recommend for anyone in the mood for an epic dark paranormal series! <br />Warning for all three books: Non-Consensual sex, violence, torture, MF, MMM, MM etc. </i>
</b><br /><br /><b> This review is for all three books, <u>first book</u> 4.25 Stars, <u>second and third books</u> 5 Stars </b> </span>
  <a data-text-id="12802096239403288234" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
